info:Deluxe Room

info:Business travelers
info:8 Reviews

posted:Posted June 5, 2024
msg:Conclusion:
1. For those who have trouble sleeping, never book a lake view room, facing the main road and the viaduct, it will be very noisy.
2. The hotel is very good at deceiving people.
The specific process of deceiving people.
1. When I checked in, I asked not to face the street. The front desk replied that I booked a lake view room, as long as it has the word "lake view", it is facing the street. I thought it was my own problem and the order could not be cancelled, so I gave up.
2. I slept very badly at night. I got up to check my order, and the room type I booked did not have the word "lake view" at all
3. When I checked out, I consulted the front desk again, and the front desk told me that I did not book a lake view room, but a quiet room facing the inside. Because the room type I booked last night was no longer available, I was upgraded to a lake view room for free.
It was obvious that the hotel had no rooms. They deceived me twice.
The first time they deceived me, they told me: I booked a lake view room
The second time they deceived me, they told me: It was a free upgrade, I should thank the hotel. Little did I know that I clearly mentioned my needs when I checked in.
Summary: Through precise words, customers are guided to accept the scam.

This complaint is to the front desk. The hotel's environment, cleaning and sanitation are all up to standard.
I hope everyone will not be deceived again.
